  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8ec11697-4e54-4b9d-915f-4a32023c41ea'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer496682374048593996"><i>A Minor Spoiler for Book 1</i><br/><br/><br/><br/>Standing on a dumpster and surrounded by zombies, Peter watched the people who had become his family drive away. He laid down his life so they could live. <br/><br/>Then just when he was about to use his last bullet and end it all, a window opens and a ladder appears. <br/><br/>At 70 pages, <i>So Long, Lollipops</i> is a fairly short novella taking up Peter's story from when his new family drove away until they are reunited. I'm a bit ambivalent about the whole zombie genre...there are things I l</span>
  <span id="freeText496682374048593996" style="display:none"><i>A Minor Spoiler for Book 1</i><br /><br /><br /><br />Standing on a dumpster and surrounded by zombies, Peter watched the people who had become his family drive away. He laid down his life so they could live. <br /><br />Then just when he was about to use his last bullet and end it all, a window opens and a ladder appears. <br /><br />At 70 pages, <i>So Long, Lollipops</i> is a fairly short novella taking up Peter's story from when his new family drove away until they are reunited. I'm a bit ambivalent about the whole zombie genre...there are things I love and things that really bug me. Not with this little story, I have no reservations at all. It's pretty damned good.</span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/23211056-so-long-lollipops">review of another edition</a>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2168548052" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer386954512888382192">This review can also be found at <a href='http://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br/><br/>I really need to warn anyone planning to read the first book in the series, Until the End of the World, to stop reading this review now. I cannot talk about this novella without spoiling the first book. It just cannot be done. This review could ruin one of the best moments in the first novel. You have been warned.<br/><br/>I enjoyed this novella quite a bit. I usually listen to audiobooks at work and only rarely listen to much at home. I decid</span>
  <span id="freeText386954512888382192" style="display:none">This review can also be found at <a href="http://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br /><br />I really need to warn anyone planning to read the first book in the series, Until the End of the World, to stop reading this review now. I cannot talk about this novella without spoiling the first book. It just cannot be done. This review could ruin one of the best moments in the first novel. You have been warned.<br /><br />I enjoyed this novella quite a bit. I usually listen to audiobooks at work and only rarely listen to much at home. I decided to start this one on a Saturday while I was walking my dogs and planned to finish during the work week. I listened to the whole thing over the weekend because I couldn't get enough. It is rather short but it answered a lot of questions that I had from the first book in the series.<br /><br />**Spoilers Ahead**<br /><br />This novella tells Peter's story. Peter was a character that I wanted to feed to the zombies at the beginning of the series. You know, the one guy that you kind of hope will die quickly and painfully. Peter did what few characters are able to do. He completely redeemed himself in the first book. The same guy I wanted to see die a horrible death became a man that I got a little choked up over once I believed he had actually met that fate. Not to mention the surprise and joy when I realized he had survived at the close of the first book.<br /><br />Since finishing Until the End of the World, I wondered how Peter could have possibly survived. When the group left him, he was in an impossible situation. This novella details what Peter goes through from the point the group left him until he is reunited and what a story it is. Peter has turned into a genuinely good guy that I would want fighting on my side. He encounters a few new characters and has some great moments with them. He also runs into more than a few zombies and things look dire a time or two. Of course, I knew he would survive and make it back to the group since I saw that in the first book from Cassie's point of view.<br /><br />I think that Julia Whelan does a great job with this series. I am very happy to see that she narrates all of the books in the series. I think it would have been a huge mistake to switch to a male narrator for this one despite the fact that this story is told from a male point of view. She does a great job with Peter and all of the other characters he encounters. I look forward to listening to this narrator again very soon.<br /><br />I would recommend this book to others. This is a series that really should be read in order. I think it would be possible to read and enjoy this as a stand alone but I don't think that it could possibly have the same kind of impact. I can't wait to read the rest of this touching zombie series!<br /><br /><b>Initial Thoughts</b><br />So this answers the question in regards to what actually happened to Peter. I am really enjoying this series now that zombies are everywhere. I picked this one up as a freebie on Audible a while back but decided to listen to them in order which I think was a good choice. This could possibly work as a stand alone but so much of the book is directly related to the first that I do think it would be best to read this series in order. I thought that the narration was very well done.<br /><br />Book source: Audible freebie</span>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1395950530" />
    <a title="Jason Parent" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11708867-jason-parent"><img alt="Jason Parent" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1447218697p2/11708867.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1395950530?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jason Parent" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jason Parent" href="/user/show/11708867-jason-parent">Jason Parent</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1395950530" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8921822393507323733">This novella was free as an audiobook on Audible, and even though it warned me that I should read the first story in the series first, I went ahead and picked it up... and felt it worked perfectly fine as its own story. In the vein of The Walking Dead and The Last of Us, though with a more positive outlook on humanity and its perseverance, So Long, Lollipops follows Peter's journey to reunite with his zombie apocalypse family after selflessly attempting to sacrifice himself to save said family. </span>
  <span id="freeText8921822393507323733" style="display:none">This novella was free as an audiobook on Audible, and even though it warned me that I should read the first story in the series first, I went ahead and picked it up... and felt it worked perfectly fine as its own story. In the vein of The Walking Dead and The Last of Us, though with a more positive outlook on humanity and its perseverance, So Long, Lollipops follows Peter's journey to reunite with his zombie apocalypse family after selflessly attempting to sacrifice himself to save said family. His journey doesn't take him far, but when your facing off with hungry zombies and desperate men, meters can seem like miles and miles, well, they can seem like forever.<br /><br />Well written, well characterized, and well plotted, this one is worth a listen. The protagonist has grown off-page and continues to grow on-page, one worth following. These elements are what separate it from otherwise typical zombie action.</span>

<div id="review_1169240433" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14548053-ambs?shelf=audible-all">audible-all</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1169240433" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3171699817009385021">Nice quick read. Story was written just as well as <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23121237-until-the-end-of-the-world' rel='nofollow noopener'>Until the End of the World</a>. <br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7171979.Sarah_Lyons_Fleming' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sarah Lyons Fleming</a> expanded on the already introduced Peter and made him more personable - something we didn't really see before because he was a secondary character (in my reference, we didn't get to hear things from his point of view). We also feel connected to some of the people he meets along the way. <br/><br/>This would be easy enough as a stand alone story, and was a great accompaniment to the series. Check it out if yo</span>
  <span id="freeText3171699817009385021" style="display:none">Nice quick read. Story was written just as well as <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23121237-until-the-end-of-the-world" rel="nofollow noopener">Until the End of the World</a>. <br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7171979.Sarah_Lyons_Fleming" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah Lyons Fleming</a> expanded on the already introduced Peter and made him more personable - something we didn't really see before because he was a secondary character (in my reference, we didn't get to hear things from his point of view). We also feel connected to some of the people he meets along the way. <br /><br />This would be easy enough as a stand alone story, and was a great accompaniment to the series. Check it out if you have a chance.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3171699817009385021" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2765960102" />
    <a title="Martha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1593142-martha"><img alt="Martha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1223843868p2/1593142.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2765960102?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Martha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Martha" href="/user/show/1593142-martha">Martha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/26875412-so-long-lollipops">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2765960102" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9850984218540888935">I enjoyed this novella telling Peter’s story after sacrifice.<br/><br/>At the end of Book 1, Until the End of the World, Peter agreed to distract the ‘zombies’ so the rest of his friends (now ‘family’) could escape to continue their trip to a safe zone community further north. Peter knows he is giving up his life, but he isn’t going down without a fight. Then he gets rescued by a young teen. Now he faces her gun but at least he is away from the “Z” mob.<br/><br/>Nat and her family are hesitant to trust Peter but Na</span>
  <span id="freeText9850984218540888935" style="display:none">I enjoyed this novella telling Peter’s story after sacrifice.<br /><br />At the end of Book 1, Until the End of the World, Peter agreed to distract the ‘zombies’ so the rest of his friends (now ‘family’) could escape to continue their trip to a safe zone community further north. Peter knows he is giving up his life, but he isn’t going down without a fight. Then he gets rescued by a young teen. Now he faces her gun but at least he is away from the “Z” mob.<br /><br />Nat and her family are hesitant to trust Peter but Nat saw how he reacted as he let “Bits” and the others drive away. After Peter suffers an accident, he has no choice but to stay with the family and help them settle into their safe house. Peter also has time to contemplate his shallow past and what it takes now to survive.<br /><br />Finally Peter sets off on his trip to the safe zone. He starts in a truck, but he has a long journey even if it isn’t that many miles. There are more enemies than just Zombies along the way but he is determined to catch up with Cassie and the others.<br /><br />I enjoyed this short story from Peter’s perspective. I liked the phrase and title “So Long Lollipops”. This tale had danger and some ‘end of the world’ thought processes. Now I am ready to get the next book in the series.<br /><br />Audio Notes: Julia Whelan continues the good job of narration for the characters in this series. She adds comfortable pacing, even with Peter’s introspective moments. I like listening to this series.<br /><br />Source: Audible Free Title 9/2014. </span>

        <a title="Mandy (I Read Indie) Anderson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandy (I Read Indie) Anderson" href="/user/show/3261049-mandy-i-read-indie-anderson">Mandy (I Read Indie) Anderson</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2269326528" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14719031285453377864">DO NOT READ MY REVIEW IF YOU HAVE NOT READ BOOK, UNTIL THE END OF THE WORLD!!!! You have been warned!!<br/>*<br/>*<br/>*<br/>*<br/>*<br/>If you have read the first book you know that Peter dies. Well his family thought he died but in all reality he was saved. I guess you can say it was a Dumpster Glenn move (The Walking Dead). But Peter’s saving was a bit more realistic. Like for real. Don't get me started on Glenn's resurrection moment. <br/><br/>At the end of book one Peter makes it back to his family and it is a wonderful reunion. </span>
  <span id="freeText14719031285453377864" style="display:none">DO NOT READ MY REVIEW IF YOU HAVE NOT READ BOOK, UNTIL THE END OF THE WORLD!!!! You have been warned!!<br />*<br />*<br />*<br />*<br />*<br />If you have read the first book you know that Peter dies. Well his family thought he died but in all reality he was saved. I guess you can say it was a Dumpster Glenn move (The Walking Dead). But Peter’s saving was a bit more realistic. Like for real. Don't get me started on Glenn's resurrection moment. <br /><br />At the end of book one Peter makes it back to his family and it is a wonderful reunion. But this book is all about what Peter endured on his journey back to them and to Kingdom Come. And it ain’t pretty. There were many close calls with the Lexers and thoughts about giving up. Several moments had me catching my breath, only to remember he made it and was safe. For the present time being at least. <br /><br />SO LONG, LOLLIPOPS was surprising yet fantastic short read. I didn’t realize until I read it how much I was interested in knowing what happened with Peter. Even though I didn’t care much for him in the beginning of book one, he really grew on me and even more so in this one. 5 Stars!<br /></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3461061431" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1740280256" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12192965566040903174">This tells Peter's story, and should not be read until you have read the first book.<br/><br/>Peter was a selfish, spoilt brat. A very well written, unlikable character, and you feel exactly the same for him as Cassie does. But even the least likely people have moments of redemption.<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ In book one, Peter shows that he can be strong for others, when he does his Dickens moment (It is a far, far better thing...) and sacrifices himself so that the others might live. We of course learn at the end </span></span>
  <span id="freeText12192965566040903174" style="display:none">This tells Peter's story, and should not be read until you have read the first book.<br /><br />Peter was a selfish, spoilt brat. A very well written, unlikable character, and you feel exactly the same for him as Cassie does. But even the least likely people have moments of redemption.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ In book one, Peter shows that he can be strong for others, when he does his Dickens moment (It is a far, far better thing...) and sacrifices himself so that the others might live. We of course learn at the end of the book that something amazing happened as he didn't have to use that final bullet on himself - this novella fills in those gaps.<br /><br />It is an incredibly worthy novella, as well written as the first book, and instead of being a filler, or detracting from what the mind can imagine, it brings another dimension to the group. Peter's growth as a character is spectacular, and yet totally believable. That he has so much more to give is a gift to the reader, as you know that he brings an interesting dynamic to the group.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1267665511?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily" href="/user/show/11168164-emily">Emily</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1267665511" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16020023544745936536">Ha, did I just claim that <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18586621.Until_the_End_of_the_World__Until_the_End_of_the_World___1_' title='Until the End of the World (Until the End of the World, #1) by Sarah Lyons Fleming' rel='nofollow noopener'> Until the End of the World</a> was too long? I know, I know. I thought this one was too short, mostly because the last part of its space is actually devoted to a chapter of another book, and so the story cut out sooner than I anticipated. <br/><br/>Other issues: First, I wanted to knock Peter over the head when he couldn't piece together where to find water (so obvious!!), and second, I would like to mention that Nelly does not drink Pepsi. Oh, sure you can buy Pepsi in Texas, but w</span>
  <span id="freeText16020023544745936536" style="display:none">Ha, did I just claim that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18586621.Until_the_End_of_the_World__Until_the_End_of_the_World___1_" title="Until the End of the World (Until the End of the World, #1) by Sarah Lyons Fleming" rel="nofollow noopener"> Until the End of the World</a> was too long? I know, I know. I thought this one was too short, mostly because the last part of its space is actually devoted to a chapter of another book, and so the story cut out sooner than I anticipated. <br /><br />Other issues: First, I wanted to knock Peter over the head when he couldn't piece together where to find water (so obvious!!), and second, I would like to mention that Nelly does not drink Pepsi. Oh, sure you can buy Pepsi in Texas, but we call it Coke down here for a reason, with the only acceptable alternative being Dr. Pepper. Nelly was not longing for a Pepsi, and I demand that it be changed for future editions.<br /><br />-----<br /><br />I recently re-read this, and the point stands. In argument that Nelly drinks Coke or DP, I report this recent conversation.<br /><br />Me: When you went on that drink run yesterday, what did you get?<br />Co-worker: You mean the Cokes?<br />Me: Yeah.<br />Co-worker: Three Dr. Peppers and two Diet Dr. Peppers. <br /><br />Drinking Dr. Pepper is like the most Texas thing. Other impressions? It still felt too short, and this time Peter not figuring out the water quickly made sense to me due to the dehydration. I wonder if I was less worried because I knew he'd find it? If there's something to say about Fleming, it's that she really makes you care about the characters. <br /><br /></span>

          </span>

I am sitting here still suffering from Until the End of the World hangover, so when I saw there was a tie-in Novella to sate my unquenchable thirst for the next book in the series, I happily downloaded it!   <span id="freeText17872941183480342373" style="display:none">Loved this book! I just LOVED it! I am sitting here still suffering from Until the End of the World hangover, so when I saw there was a tie-in Novella to sate my unquenchable thirst for the next book in the series, I happily downloaded it! I would NOT read this book until you read Until The End of the World first though! This book was just what the readers needed I think to get a glimpse of Peter and really why he is the way that he was! It's funny how he was one of my LEAST favorite characters in this series....but as time went on, my heart just melts for him! I just love how Mrs. Fleming was able to bring this character out of the darkness, and make him shine like the Hero he was meant to be! I can not wait until the next book in the series! </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1550168095978704289">I haven't listened to the series but the way this story is written seems like a side story about a character from something larger. It was entertaining but I can't say I really got into it. The writing was good, the narration was great and usually this is the type of story I love, however this one didn't make me go wow! <br/><br/>I like to feel the characters dilemna and I can't say I really felt for Peter. At times I did as he battled zombies and was at times in situations that couldn't get much worse. T</span>
  <span id="freeText1550168095978704289" style="display:none">I haven't listened to the series but the way this story is written seems like a side story about a character from something larger. It was entertaining but I can't say I really got into it. The writing was good, the narration was great and usually this is the type of story I love, however this one didn't make me go wow! <br /><br />I like to feel the characters dilemna and I can't say I really felt for Peter. At times I did as he battled zombies and was at times in situations that couldn't get much worse. The author didn't drag me into his mind and struggle. It was decent though and the series it belongs to might be a stronger read. </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('fWfuyDY4psDFSJgczNCWPz7w6LbUgWeNZ9umR7i6uLEoTfzXxjq45xMV0zPi16VaaNOn9ewuXLzgMXlsTkOVtg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EZ7viJAgesC9hVdr0m1aJ5BySaJpG3Szy3A1q043JgFEtP2XYCJk52vYHET8amlCxlEG4VG0T4JMmuqAuM4LBg==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText11001975078812868142" style="display:none">I'm a Laura Ingalls devotee, wannabe prepper and lover of anything pre-apocalyptic, apocalyptic and post-apocalyptic—-or anything in between. Born and raised in Brooklyn, NY, I now live in Oregon with my family and, in my opinion, not nearly enough supplies for the zombie apocalypse. But I'm working on it.<br /></span>
